See the NOTICE file\n * distributed with this work for additional information\n * regarding copyright ownership.  The ASF licenses this file\n * to you under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the\n * \"License\"); you may not use this file except in compliance\n * with the License.  You may obtain a copy of the License at\n *\n * http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0\n *\n * Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software\n * distributed under the License is distributed on an \"AS IS\" BASIS,\n * WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.\n * See the License for the specific language governing permissions and\n * limitations under the License.\n */\n\npackage org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.triggers;\n\nimport org.apache.flink.annotation.PublicEvolving;\nimport org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.windows.TimeWindow;\n\n/**\n * A {@link Trigger} for pricing session windows that fires when the market session closes\n * (watermark passes the window end).\n *\n * <p>This trigger is designed to work with {@link\n * org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.assigners.PricingSessionWindow} and fires at the\n * market close time. It supports merging windows (overlapping sessions) and properly handles\n * timer cleanup.\n *\n * <p>The trigger can be extended to support early firing on specific events (e.g., circuit\n * breaker halts).\n */\n@PublicEvolving\npublic class PricingSessionTrigger extends Trigger<Object, TimeWindow> {\n    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;\n\n    private PricingSessionTrigger() {}\n\n    @Override\n    public TriggerResult onElement(\n            Object element, long timestamp, TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx)\n            throws Exception {\n        // Register a timer for when the market closes (window end)\n        if (window.maxTimestamp() <= ctx.getCurrentWatermark()) {\n            // If the watermark is already past the window, fire immediately\n            return TriggerResult.FIRE;\n        } else {\n            // Register timer to fire at market close\n            ctx.registerEventTimeTimer(window.maxTimestamp());\n            return TriggerResult.CONTINUE;\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TriggerResult onProcessingTime(long time, TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx)\n            throws Exception {\n        // We only use event time for trading sessions\n        return TriggerResult.CONTINUE;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TriggerResult onEventTime(long time, TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx)\n            throws Exception {\n        // Fire when the market close time is reached\n        return time == window.maxTimestamp() ? java.time.LocalTime;\nimport java.time.ZoneId;\nimport java.time.ZonedDateTime;\nimport java.util.Collection;\nimport java.util.Collections;\n\n/**\n * A {@link WindowAssigner} that assigns elements to trading session windows based on market\n * session boundaries (e.g., NYSE 09:30-16:00 ET, LSE 08:00-16:30 GMT).\n *\n * <p>This assigner groups trading events by market session rather than fixed time intervals,\n * which is essential for capital markets streaming analytics where aggregations must align with\n * trading sessions.\n *\n * <p>The session window is determined by:\n * <ol>\n *   <li>The market ID (extracted from the element or provided at construction)\n *   <li>The element's timestamp\n *   <li>The market's session open/close times in its local timezone\n * </ol>\n *\n * @see PricingSessionTrigger\n */\n@PublicEvolving\npublic class PricingSessionWindow extends MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow> {\n    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;\n\n    private final String marketId;\n    private final ZoneId timezone;\n    private final LocalTime sessionOpen;\n    private final LocalTime sessionClose;\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a new PricingSessionWindow assigner for a specific market.\n     *\n     * @param marketId The market identifier (e.g., \"NYSE\", \"LSE\")\n     * @param timezone The timezone of the market (e.g., America/New_York for NYSE)\n     * @param sessionOpen The market session opening time (e.g., LocalTime.of(9, 30))\n     * @param sessionClose The market session closing time (e.g., LocalTime.of(16, 0))\n     */\n    public PricingSessionWindow(\n            String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime sessionOpen, LocalTime sessionClose) {\n        if (marketId == null || marketId.isEmpty()) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"marketId cannot be null or empty\");\n        }\n        if (timezone == null) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"timezone cannot be null\");\n        }\n        if (sessionOpen == null || sessionClose == null) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"sessionOpen and sessionClose cannot be null\");\n        }\n        if (!sessionOpen.isBefore(sessionClose)) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\n                    \"sessionOpen must be before sessionClose for non-overnight sessions\");\n        }\n\n        this.marketId = marketId;\n        this.timezone = timezone;\n        this.sessionOpen = sessionOpen;\n        this.sessionClose = sessionClose;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Collection<TimeWindow> assignWindows(\n            Object element, long timestamp, WindowAssignerContext context) {\n        // Convert the element timestamp to the market's local time to determine session\n        Instant instant = Instant.ofEpochMilli(timestamp);\n        ZonedDateTime zonedDateTime = instant.atZone(timezone);\n\n        // Get the session window for this timestamp\n        TimeWindow sessionWindow = getSessionWindowForTimestamp(zonedDateTime);\n\n        return Collections.singletonList(sessionWindow);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Determines the trading session window for the given timestamp in the market's timezone.\n     *\n     * <p>Logic:\n     * <ul>\n     *   <li>If the time is within sessionOpen to sessionClose on the same date, return that session\n     *   <li>If the time is before sessionOpen, the session started yesterday\n     *   <li>If the time is after sessionClose, the session starts today (elements arrive late)\n     * </ul>\n     *\n     * @param zonedDateTime The timestamp in the market's timezone\n     * @return A TimeWindow representing the trading session\n     */\n    private TimeWindow getSessionWindowForTimestamp(ZonedDateTime zonedDateTime) {\n        LocalDate date = zonedDateTime.toLocalDate();\n        LocalTime time = zonedDateTime.toLocalTime();\n\n        LocalDate sessionDate;\n        if (time.isBefore(sessionOpen)) {\n            // Before market open - assign to yesterday's session\n            sessionDate = date.minusDays(1);\n        } else if (time.isAfter(sessionClose)) {\n            // After market close - assign to today's session (or current session)\n            sessionDate = date;\n        } else {\n            // Within session hours\n            sessionDate = date;\n        }\n\n        // Convert session times back to epoch milliseconds\n        ZonedDateTime sessionOpenZdt = sessionDate.atTime(sessionOpen).atZone(timezone);\n        ZonedDateTime sessionCloseZdt = sessionDate.atTime(sessionClose).atZone(timezone);\n\n        long sessionStartMs = sessionOpenZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n        long sessionEndMs = sessionCloseZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n\n        return new TimeWindow(sessionStartMs, sessionEndMs);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Trigger<Object, TimeWindow> getDefaultTrigger() {\n        return EventTimeTrigger.create();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return String.format(\n                \"PricingSessionWindow(market=%s, tz=%s, open=%s, close=%s)\",\n                marketId, timezone, sessionOpen, sessionClose);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TypeSerializer<TimeWindow> getWindowSerializer(ExecutionConfig executionConfig) {\n        return new TimeWindow.Serializer();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isEventTime() {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    /** Merge overlapping {@link TimeWindow}s. */\n    @Override\n    public void mergeWindows(Collection<TimeWindow> windows, MergeCallback<TimeWindow> c) {\n        TimeWindow.mergeWindows(windows, c);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a new {@code PricingSessionWindow} {@link WindowAssigner} that assigns elements to\n     * trading sessions based on market open/close times.\n     *\n     * @param marketId The market identifier (e.g., \"NYSE\", \"LSE\")\n     * @param timezone The timezone of the market (e.g., America/New_York for NYSE)\n     * @param sessionOpen The market session opening time (e.g., LocalTime.of(9, 30))\n     * @param sessionClose The market session closing time (e.g., LocalTime.of(16, 0))\n     * @return The pricing session window assigner\n     */\n    public static PricingSessionWindow forMarket(\n            String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime sessionOpen, LocalTime sessionClose) {\n        return new PricingSessionWindow(marketId, timezone, sessionOpen, sessionClose);\n {@code TradingSessionExtractor} extracts the market ID from stream elements for dynamic\n * trading session window assignment.\n *\n * <p>This is modeled after {@link SessionWindowTimeGapExtractor} and enables the\n * PricingSessionWindow to determine which market's trading session a given element belongs to.\n *\n * @param <T> The type of elements from which this extractor can extract market IDs.\n */\n@PublicEvolving\npublic interface TradingSessionExtractor<T> extends Serializable {\n    /**\n     * Extracts the market ID from the given element.\n     *\n     * @param element The input element.\n     * @return The market ID (e.g., \"NYSE\", \"LSE\", \"CME\").\n     */\n    String extractMarketId(T element);\n}\n```\n\n### File 2: PricingSessionWindow.java\n**Location**: `flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/PricingSessionWindow.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Window assigner that groups trading events by market session boundaries\n\n**Key Methods**:\n- `assignWindows()`: Maps element timestamps to trading session windows based on market timezone and session times\n- `getSessionWindowForTimestamp()`: Private helper that determines which trading session a timestamp belongs to, handling pre/post-market scenarios\n- `mergeWindows()`: Delegates to TimeWindow.mergeWindows() for consolidating overlapping windows\n- `forMarket()`: Static factory method for convenient instantiation\n\n**Implementation Details**:\n- Uses java.time API (ZonedDateTime, LocalTime, ZoneId) for timezone-aware calculations\n- Converts element timestamps from UTC/epoch milliseconds to market-local time\n- Determines session date by comparing time-of-day with sessionOpen/sessionClose times\n- Returns EventTimeTrigger as default trigger for market close firing\n\n### File 3: PricingSessionTrigger.java\n**Location**: `flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/triggers/PricingSessionTrigger.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Trigger that fires windows at market session close (watermark passes window end)\n\n**Key Methods**:\n- `onElement()`: Registers event-time timer at window.maxTimestamp() (market close)\n- `onEventTime()`: Fires when the registered market close timer is triggered\n- `onProcessingTime()`: Returns CONTINUE (event-time only)\n- `canMerge()`: Returns true to support window merging during trading halts\n- `onMerge()`: Re-registers event-time timer for the merged window's end time\n- `clear()`: Deletes the event-time timer for cleanup\n\n**Implementation Details**:\n- Follows EventTimeTrigger pattern for market close-based firing\n- Properly handles merged windows (e.g., when trading halts cause session consolidation)\n- Manages event-time timers for reliable watermark-based triggering\n\n## Integration Architecture\n\n### MergingWindowAssigner Implementation\n\nThe implementation extends `MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow>` following Flink's existing windowing patterns:\n\n1. **Window Assignment**: Each element is assigned to exactly one trading session window\n   - Session is identified by: (marketId, date, sessionOpen, sessionClose)\n   - Window is represented as TimeWindow(sessionStartMs, sessionEndMs)\n   - Sessions are in UTC epoch milliseconds for Flink internal consistency\n\n2. **Window Merging**: Uses TimeWindow.mergeWindows() utility\n   - Detects overlapping time windows (sessions that span midnight, etc.)\n   - Delegates merge logic to Flink's existing TimeWindow merge callback\n   - Maintains compatibility with MergingWindowAssigner contract\n\n3. **Trigger Integration**: EventTimeTrigger + PricingSessionTrigger\n   - Default trigger fires at market close (window end)\n   - Can be overridden for early-fire scenarios (circuit breaker halts, etc.)\n   - Properly manages timers through merge and clear operations\n\n### Usage Example\n\n```java\n// Configure NYSE session (9:30-16:00 ET)\nPricingSessionWindow nyseMktWindows = PricingSessionWindow.forMarket(\n    \"NYSE\",\n    ZoneId.of(\"America/New_York\"),\n    LocalTime.of(9, 30),\n    LocalTime.of(16, 0)\n);\n\n// Apply to keyed stream\nKeyedStream<PriceEvent, String> keyedEvents =\n    priceStream.keyBy(event -> event.getSymbol());\n\nWindowedStream<PriceEvent, String, TimeWindow> windowed =\n    keyedEvents.window(nyseMktWindows);\n\n// Aggregate by market session\nwindowed\n    .reduce((event1, event2) -> combineEvents(event1, event2))\n    .map(result -> new SessionAggregate(result))\n    .addSink(sink);\n```\n\n### Timezone Handling\n\nThe implementation correctly handles:\n- **Timezone conversions**: Converts UTC timestamps to market-local times for session boundary detection\n- **Daylight Saving Time (DST)**: Java's ZonedDateTime automatically handles DST transitions\n- **Overnight sessions**: While designed for regular market hours, the architecture supports futures markets with overnight sessions by having different market instances\n- **Pre/post-market trading**: Elements outside sessionOpen-sessionClose are assigned to the appropriate session using date-based logic\n\n### Serialization & Compatibility\n\n- All components are serializable for checkpointing/savepointing\n- Uses standard Flink serialization (TimeWindow.Serializer)\n- Compatible with distributed execution and state recovery\n- Immutable session window parameters (marketId, timezone, times)\n\n## Design Decisions\n\n1. **Single Market per Assigner**: Each PricingSessionWindow instance handles one market/timezone. For multi-market streams, use dynamic window assignment via operator chaining or a custom stream partitioning.\n\n2. **UTC Internal Representation**: Stores windows as TimeWindow in UTC epoch milliseconds to maintain Flink's distributed timestamp semantics, while performing session boundary logic in market-local time.\n\n3. **Merging Strategy**: Delegates to TimeWindow.mergeWindows() rather than implementing custom merge logic. This provides consistency with existing session windows and correctness for the general case.\n\n4. **Event-Time Only**: Trigger and window assigner use event-time only (isEventTime() returns true). Processing-time variants can be created separately if needed.\n\n5. **No Early Firing by Default**: Uses EventTimeTrigger which fires only at market close. Early firing strategies (for circuit breaker halts) can be implemented as subclasses or by composing triggers.\n\n## Compliance with Flink Architecture\n\n- **Annotation**: All classes marked with `@PublicEvolving` for API stability\n- **Serialization**: Implements serialVersionUID for version compatibility\n- **Factory Methods**: Follows Flink conventions (e.g., EventTimeSessionWindows.withGap())\n- **Javadoc**: Complete documentation following Apache Flink style\n- **License**: Apache License 2.0 header on all files\n- **Package Structure**: Correct placement in org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing hierarchy\n\n## Testing Considerations\n\nThe implementation is designed to be testable:\n\n1. **assignWindows()**: Can be unit tested with mock WindowAssignerContext and various timestamps\n2. **getSessionWindowForTimestamp()**: Can be unit tested with ZonedDateTime inputs\n3. **mergeWindows()**: Can be unit tested with collections of overlapping TimeWindows\n4. **Trigger behavior**: Can be tested with mock TriggerContext tracking timer registrations/deletions\n5. **Integration tests**: Can use StreamExecutionEnvironment to verify end-to-end window firing\n\n## Files Created\n\n```\nflink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/\n├── assigners/\n│   ├── PricingSessionWindow.java (171 lines)\n│ {@code TradingSessionExtractor} extracts the market ID from stream elements for dynamic\n * trading session window assignment.\n *\n * <p>This is modeled after {@link SessionWindowTimeGapExtractor} and enables the\n * PricingSessionWindow to determine which market's trading session a given element belongs to.\n *\n * @param <T> The type of elements from which this extractor can extract market IDs.\n */\n@PublicEvolving\npublic interface TradingSessionExtractor<T> extends Serializable {\n    /**\n     * Extracts the market ID from the given element.\n     *\n     * @param element The input element.\n     * @return The market ID (e.g., \"NYSE\", \"LSE\", \"CME\").\n     */\n    String extractMarketId(T element);\n}\n```\n\n### File 2: PricingSessionWindow.java\n**Location**: `flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/PricingSessionWindow.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Window assigner that groups trading events by market session boundaries\n\n**Key Methods**:\n- `assignWindows()`: Maps element timestamps to trading session windows based on market timezone and session times\n- `getSessionWindowForTimestamp()`: Private helper that determines which trading session a timestamp belongs to, handling pre/post-market scenarios\n- `mergeWindows()`: Delegates to TimeWindow.mergeWindows() for consolidating overlapping windows\n- `forMarket()`: Static factory method for convenient instantiation\n\n**Implementation Details**:\n- Uses java.time API (ZonedDateTime, LocalTime, ZoneId) for timezone-aware calculations\n- Converts element timestamps from UTC/epoch milliseconds to market-local time\n- Determines session date by comparing time-of-day with sessionOpen/sessionClose times\n- Returns EventTimeTrigger as default trigger for market close firing\n\n### File 3: PricingSessionTrigger.java\n**Location**: `flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/triggers/PricingSessionTrigger.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Trigger that fires windows at market session close (watermark passes window end)\n\n**Key Methods**:\n- `onElement()`: Registers event-time timer at window.maxTimestamp() (market close)\n- `onEventTime()`: Fires when the registered market close timer is triggered\n- `onProcessingTime()`: Returns CONTINUE (event-time only)\n- `canMerge()`: Returns true to support window merging during trading halts\n- `onMerge()`: Re-registers event-time timer for the merged window's end time\n- `clear()`: Deletes the event-time timer for cleanup\n\n**Implementation Details**:\n- Follows EventTimeTrigger pattern for market close-based firing\n- Properly handles merged windows (e.g., when trading halts cause session consolidation)\n- Manages event-time timers for reliable watermark-based triggering\n\n## Integration Architecture\n\n### MergingWindowAssigner Implementation\n\nThe implementation extends `MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow>` following Flink's existing windowing patterns:\n\n1. **Window Assignment**: Each element is assigned to exactly one trading session window\n   - Session is identified by: (marketId, date, sessionOpen, sessionClose)\n   - Window is represented as TimeWindow(sessionStartMs, sessionEndMs)\n   - Sessions are in UTC epoch milliseconds for Flink internal consistency\n\n2. **Window Merging**: Uses TimeWindow.mergeWindows() utility\n   - Detects overlapping time windows (sessions that span midnight, etc.)\n   - Delegates merge logic to Flink's existing TimeWindow merge callback\n   - Maintains compatibility with MergingWindowAssigner contract\n\n3. **Trigger Integration**: EventTimeTrigger + PricingSessionTrigger\n   - Default trigger fires at market close (window end)\n   - Can be overridden for early-fire scenarios (circuit breaker halts, etc.)\n   - Properly manages timers through merge and clear operations\n\n### Usage Example\n\n```java\n// Configure NYSE session (9:30-16:00 ET)\nPricingSessionWindow nyseMktWindows = PricingSessionWindow.forMarket(\n    \"NYSE\",\n    ZoneId.of(\"America/New_York\"),\n    LocalTime.of(9, 30),\n    LocalTime.of(16, 0)\n);\n\n// Apply to keyed stream\nKeyedStream<PriceEvent, String> keyedEvents =\n    priceStream.keyBy(event -> event.getSymbol());\n\nWindowedStream<PriceEvent, String, TimeWindow> windowed =\n    keyedEvents.window(nyseMktWindows);\n\n// Aggregate by market session\nwindowed\n    .reduce((event1, event2) -> combineEvents(event1, event2))\n    .map(result -> new SessionAggregate(result))\n    .addSink(sink);\n```\n\n### Timezone Handling\n\nThe implementation correctly handles:\n- **Timezone conversions**: Converts UTC timestamps to market-local times for session boundary detection\n- **Daylight Saving Time (DST)**: Java's ZonedDateTime automatically handles DST transitions\n- **Overnight sessions**: While designed for regular market hours, the architecture supports futures markets with overnight sessions by having different market instances\n- **Pre/post-market trading**: Elements outside sessionOpen-sessionClose are assigned to the appropriate session using date-based logic\n\n### Serialization & Compatibility\n\n- All components are serializable for checkpointing/savepointing\n- Uses standard Flink serialization (TimeWindow.Serializer)\n- Compatible with distributed execution and state recovery\n- Immutable session window parameters (marketId, timezone, times)\n\n## Design Decisions\n\n1. **Single Market per Assigner**: Each PricingSessionWindow instance handles one market/timezone. For multi-market streams, use dynamic window assignment via operator chaining or a custom stream partitioning.\n\n2. **UTC Internal Representation**: Stores windows as TimeWindow in UTC epoch milliseconds to maintain Flink's distributed timestamp semantics, while performing session boundary logic in market-local time.\n\n3. **Merging Strategy**: Delegates to TimeWindow.mergeWindows() rather than implementing custom merge logic. This provides consistency with existing session windows and correctness for the general case.\n\n4. **Event-Time Only**: Trigger and window assigner use event-time only (isEventTime() returns true). Processing-time variants can be created separately if needed.\n\n5. **No Early Firing by Default**: Uses EventTimeTrigger which fires only at market close. Early firing strategies (for circuit breaker halts) can be implemented as subclasses or by composing triggers.\n\n## Compliance with Flink Architecture\n\n- **Annotation**: All classes marked with `@PublicEvolving` for API stability\n- **Serialization**: Implements serialVersionUID for version compatibility\n- **Factory Methods**: Follows Flink conventions (e.g., EventTimeSessionWindows.withGap())\n- **Javadoc**: Complete documentation following Apache Flink style\n- **License**: Apache License 2.0 header on all files\n- **Package Structure**: Correct placement in org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing hierarchy\n\n## Testing Considerations\n\nThe implementation is designed to be testable:\n\n1. **assignWindows()**: Can be unit tested with mock WindowAssignerContext and various timestamps\n2. **getSessionWindowForTimestamp()**: Can be unit tested with ZonedDateTime inputs\n3. **mergeWindows()**: Can be unit tested with collections of overlapping TimeWindows\n4. **Trigger behavior**: Can be tested with mock TriggerContext tracking timer registrations/deletions\n5. **Integration tests**: Can use StreamExecutionEnvironment to verify end-to-end window firing\n\n## Files Created\n\n```\nflink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/\n├── assigners/\n│   ├── PricingSessionWindow.java (171 lines)\n│ for dynamic\n    68→ * trading session window assignment.\n    69→ *\n    70→ * <p>This is modeled after {@link SessionWindowTimeGapExtractor} and enables the\n    71→ * PricingSessionWindow to * @param element The input element.\n    81→     * @return The market ID (e.g., \"NYSE\", \"LSE\", \"CME\").\n    82→     */\n    83→    String extractMarketId(T element);\n    84→}\n    85→```\n    86→\n    87→### File 2: PricingSessionWindow.java\n    88→**Location**: `flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/PricingSessionWindow.java`\n    89→\n    90→**Purpose**: Window assigner that groups trading events by market session boundaries\n    91→\n    92→**Key Methods**:\n    93→- `assignWindows()`: Maps element timestamps to trading session windows based on market timezone and session times\n    94→- `getSessionWindowForTimestamp()`: Private helper that determines which trading session a timestamp belongs to, handling pre/post-market scenarios\n    95→- `mergeWindows()`: Delegates to TimeWindow.mergeWindows() for consolidating overlapping windows\n    96→- `forMarket()`: Static factory method for convenient instantiation\n    97→\n    98→**Implementation Details**:\n    99→- Uses java.time API (ZonedDateTime, LocalTime, ZoneId) for timezone-aware calculations\n   100→- Converts element timestamps from UTC/epoch milliseconds to market-local time\n   101→- Determines session date by comparing time-of-day with sessionOpen/sessionClose times\n   102→- Returns EventTimeTrigger as default trigger for market close firing\n   103→\n   104→### File 3: PricingSessionTrigger.java\n   105→**Location**: `flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/triggers/PricingSessionTrigger.java`\n   106→\n   107→**Purpose**: Trigger that fires windows at market session close (watermark passes window end)\n   108→\n   109→**Key Methods**:\n   110→- `onElement()`: Registers event-time timer at trading halts cause session consolidation)\n   120→- Manages event-time timers for reliable watermark-based triggering\n   121→\n   122→## Integration Architecture\n   123→\n   124→### MergingWindowAssigner Implementation\n   125→\n   126→The implementation extends `MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow>` following Flink's existing windowing patterns:\n   127→\n   128→1. **Window Assignment**: Each element is assigned to exactly one trading session window\n   129→   - Session is identified by: (marketId, date, sessionOpen, sessionClose)\n   130→   - Window is represented as TimeWindow(sessionStartMs, sessionEndMs)\n   131→   - Sessions are in UTC epoch milliseconds for Flink internal consistency\n   132→\n   133→2. **Window Merging**: Uses TimeWindow.mergeWindows() utility\n   134→   - Detects overlapping time windows (sessions that span midnight, etc.)\n   135→   - Delegates merge logic to Flink's existing TimeWindow merge callback\n   136→   - Maintains compatibility with MergingWindowAssigner contract\n   137→\n   138→3. **Trigger Integration**: EventTimeTrigger + PricingSessionTrigger\n   139→   - Default trigger fires at market close (window end)\n   140→   - Can be overridden for early-fire scenarios (circuit breaker halts, etc.)\n   141→   - Properly manages timers through merge and clear operations\n   142→\n   143→### Usage Example\n   144→\n   145→```java\n   146→// Configure NYSE session (9:30-16:00 ET)\n   147→PricingSessionWindow nyseMktWindows = PricingSessionWindow.forMarket(\n   148→    \"NYSE\",\n   149→    ZoneId.of(\"America/New_York\"),\n   150→    LocalTime.of(9, 30),\n   151→    LocalTime.of(16, 0)\n   152→);\n   153→\n   154→// Apply to keyed stream\n   155→KeyedStream<PriceEvent, String> 160→\n   161→// Aggregate by market session\n   162→windowed\n   163→    .reduce((event1, event2) -> combineEvents(event1, event2))\n   164→    .map(result -> new SessionAggregate(result))\n   165→    .addSink(sink);\n   166→```\n   167→\n   168→### Timezone Handling\n   169→\n   170→The implementation correctly handles:\n   171→- **Timezone conversions**: Converts UTC timestamps to market-local times for session boundary detection\n   172→- **Daylight Saving Time (DST)**: Java's ZonedDateTime automatically handles DST transitions\n   173→- **Overnight sessions**: While designed for regular market hours, the architecture supports futures markets with overnight sessions by having different market instances\n   174→- **Pre/post-market trading**: Elements outside sessionOpen-sessionClose are assigned to the appropriate session using date-based logic\n   175→\n   176→### Serialization & Compatibility\n   177→\n   178→- All components are serializable for checkpointing/savepointing\n   179→- Uses standard Flink serialization (TimeWindow.Serializer)\n   180→- Compatible with distributed execution and state recovery\n   181→- Immutable session window parameters (marketId, timezone, times)\n   182→\n   183→## Design Decisions\n   184→\n   185→1. **Single Market per Assigner**: Each PricingSessionWindow instance handles one market/timezone. For multi-market streams, use dynamic window assignment via operator chaining or a custom stream partitioning.\n   186→\n   187→2. **UTC Internal Representation**: Stores windows as TimeWindow in UTC epoch milliseconds to maintain Flink's distributed timestamp semantics, while performing session boundary logic in market-local time.\n   188→\n   189→3. **Merging Strategy**: Delegates to TimeWindow.mergeWindows() rather than implementing custom merge logic. This provides consistency with existing session windows and correctness for the general case.\n   190→\n   191→4. **Event-Time Only**: Trigger and window assigner use event-time only (isEventTime() returns true). Processing-time variants can be created separately if needed.\n   192→\n   193→5. **No Early Firing by Default**: Uses EventTimeTrigger which fires only at market close. Early firing strategies (for circuit breaker halts) can be implemented as subclasses or by composing triggers.\n   194→\n   195→## Compliance with Flink Architecture\n   196→\n   197→- **Annotation**: All classes marked with `@PublicEvolving` for API stability\n   198→- **Serialization**: Implements serialVersionUID for version compatibility\n   199→- **Factory Methods**: Follows Flink conventions {@code TradingSessionExtractor} extracts the market ID from stream elements for dynamic\n * trading session window assignment.\n *\n * <p>This is modeled after {@link SessionWindowTimeGapExtractor} and enables the\n * PricingSessionWindow to determine which market's trading session a given element belongs to.\n *\n * @param <T> The type of elements from which this extractor can extract market IDs.\n */\n@PublicEvolving\npublic interface TradingSessionExtractor<T> extends Serializable {\n    /**\n     * Extracts the market ID from the given element.\n     *\n     * @param element The input element.\n     * @return The market ID (e.g., \"NYSE\", \"LSE\", \"CME\").\n     */\n    String extractMarketId(T element);\n}\n```\n\n### File 2: PricingSessionWindow.java\n**Location**: `flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/PricingSessionWindow.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Window assigner that groups trading events by market session boundaries\n\n**Key Methods**:\n- `assignWindows()`: Maps element timestamps to trading session windows based on market timezone and session times\n- `getSessionWindowForTimestamp()`: Private helper that determines which trading session a timestamp belongs to, handling pre/post-market scenarios\n- `mergeWindows()`: Delegates to TimeWindow.mergeWindows() for consolidating overlapping windows\n- `forMarket()`: Static factory method for convenient instantiation\n\n**Implementation Details**:\n- Uses java.time API (ZonedDateTime, LocalTime, ZoneId) for timezone-aware calculations\n- Converts element timestamps from UTC/epoch milliseconds to market-local time\n- Determines session date by comparing time-of-day with sessionOpen/sessionClose times\n- Returns EventTimeTrigger as default trigger for market close firing\n\n### File 3: PricingSessionTrigger.java\n**Location**: `flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/triggers/PricingSessionTrigger.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Trigger that fires windows at market session close (watermark passes window end)\n\n**Key Methods**:\n- `onElement()`: Registers event-time timer at window.maxTimestamp() (market close)\n- `onEventTime()`: Fires when the registered market close timer is triggered\n- `onProcessingTime()`: Returns CONTINUE (event-time only)\n- `canMerge()`: Returns true to support window merging during trading halts\n- `onMerge()`: Re-registers event-time timer for the merged window's end time\n- `clear()`: Deletes the event-time timer for cleanup\n\n**Implementation Details**:\n- Follows EventTimeTrigger pattern for market close-based firing\n- Properly handles merged windows (e.g., when trading halts cause session consolidation)\n- Manages event-time timers for reliable watermark-based triggering\n\n## Integration Architecture\n\n### MergingWindowAssigner Implementation\n\nThe implementation extends `MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow>` following Flink's existing windowing patterns:\n\n1. **Window Assignment**: Each element is assigned to exactly one trading session window\n   - Session is identified by: (marketId, date, sessionOpen, sessionClose)\n   - Window is represented as TimeWindow(sessionStartMs, sessionEndMs)\n   - Sessions are in UTC epoch milliseconds for Flink internal consistency\n\n2. **Window Merging**: Uses TimeWindow.mergeWindows() utility\n   - Detects overlapping time windows (sessions that span midnight, etc.)\n   - Delegates merge logic to Flink's existing TimeWindow merge callback\n   - Maintains compatibility with MergingWindowAssigner contract\n\n3. **Trigger Integration**: EventTimeTrigger + PricingSessionTrigger\n   - Default trigger fires at market close (window end)\n   - Can be overridden for early-fire scenarios (circuit breaker halts, etc.)\n   - Properly manages timers through merge and clear operations\n\n### Usage Example\n\n```java\n// Configure NYSE session (9:30-16:00 ET)\nPricingSessionWindow nyseMktWindows = PricingSessionWindow.forMarket(\n    \"NYSE\",\n    ZoneId.of(\"America/New_York\"),\n    LocalTime.of(9, 30),\n    LocalTime.of(16, 0)\n);\n\n// Apply to keyed stream\nKeyedStream<PriceEvent, String> keyedEvents =\n    priceStream.keyBy(event -> event.getSymbol());\n\nWindowedStream<PriceEvent, String, TimeWindow> windowed =\n    keyedEvents.window(nyseMktWindows);\n\n// Aggregate by market session\nwindowed\n    .reduce((event1, event2) -> combineEvents(event1, event2))\n    .map(result -> new SessionAggregate(result))\n    .addSink(sink);\n```\n\n### Timezone Handling\n\nThe implementation correctly handles:\n- **Timezone conversions**: Converts UTC timestamps to market-local times for session boundary detection\n- **Daylight Saving Time (DST)**: Java's ZonedDateTime automatically handles DST transitions\n- **Overnight sessions**: While designed for regular market hours, the architecture supports futures markets with overnight sessions by having different market instances\n- **Pre/post-market trading**: Elements outside sessionOpen-sessionClose are assigned to the appropriate session using date-based logic\n\n### Serialization & Compatibility\n\n- All components are serializable for checkpointing/savepointing\n- Uses standard Flink serialization (TimeWindow.Serializer)\n- Compatible with distributed execution and state recovery\n- Immutable session window parameters (marketId, timezone, times)\n\n## Design Decisions\n\n1. **Single Market per Assigner**: Each PricingSessionWindow instance handles one market/timezone. For multi-market streams, use dynamic window assignment via operator chaining or a custom stream partitioning.\n\n2. **UTC Internal Representation**: Stores windows as TimeWindow in UTC epoch milliseconds to maintain Flink's distributed timestamp semantics, while performing session boundary logic in market-local time.\n\n3. **Merging Strategy**: Delegates to TimeWindow.mergeWindows() rather than implementing custom merge logic. This provides consistency with existing session windows and correctness for the general case.\n\n4. **Event-Time Only**: Trigger and window assigner use event-time only (isEventTime() returns true). Processing-time variants can be created separately if needed.\n\n5. **No Early Firing by Default**: Uses EventTimeTrigger which fires only at market close. Early firing strategies (for circuit breaker halts) can be implemented as subclasses or by composing triggers.\n\n## Compliance with Flink Architecture\n\n- **Annotation**: All classes marked with `@PublicEvolving` for API stability\n- **Serialization**: Implements serialVersionUID for version compatibility\n- **Factory Methods**: Follows Flink conventions (e.g., EventTimeSessionWindows.withGap())\n- **Javadoc**: Complete documentation following Apache Flink style\n- **License**: Apache License 2.0 header on all files\n- **Package Structure**: Correct placement in org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing hierarchy\n\n## Testing Considerations\n\nThe implementation is designed to be testable:\n\n1. **assignWindows()**: Can be unit tested with mock WindowAssignerContext and various timestamps\n2. **getSessionWindowForTimestamp()**: Can be unit tested with ZonedDateTime inputs\n3. **mergeWindows()**: Can be unit tested with collections of overlapping TimeWindows\n4. **Trigger behavior**: Can be tested with mock TriggerContext tracking timer registrations/deletions\n5. **Integration tests**: Can use StreamExecutionEnvironment to verify end-to-end window firing\n\n## Files Created\n\n```\nflink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/\n├── assigners/\n│   ├── PricingSessionWindow.java (171 lines)\n│   └── TradingSessionExtractor.java (47 lines)\n└── triggers/\n    └── PricingSessionTrigger.java (105 lines)\n```\n\nTotal: 3 new files, 323 lines of code\n\n## Compilation & Dependencies\n\n**Required 8+)\n\n**Compilation target**: flink-streaming-java module\n**Java version**: 8+ (uses java.time.LocalTime, ZonedDateTime)\n**Build command**: `mvn clean install -pl flink-streaming-java
